  F ⟹ G)) ⟦ C, C' ⟧

D: ((λ C : univalent_category,
  disp_univalent_category C),,
 (λ (C C' : univalent_category)

D': ((λ C : univalent_category,
  disp_univalent_category C),,
 (λ (C C' : univalent_category)

C₁, C₂, C₃: univalent_category
f1, f2: C₁ ⟶ C₂
g: C₂ ⟶ C₃
r: f1 ⟹ f2
x: disp_univalent_category C₁
y: disp_univalent_category C₂
z: disp_univalent_category C₃
ff1: disp_functor f1 x y
ff2: disp_functor f2 x y
gg: disp_functor g y z
rr: disp_nat_trans r ff1 ff2
disp_nat_trans (post_whisker r g)
  (disp_functor_composite_data ff1 gg)
  (disp_functor_composite_data ff2 gg)

    exact (@post_whisker_disp_nat_trans C₁ C₂ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ rr _).
Defined.

x0: a
xx: x x0
transportf (mor_disp (ff x0 xx) (gg x0 xx))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (! id2_left η) x0)
  (ηη x0 xx) = (disp_id2 ff •• ηη) x0 xx

x0: a
xx: w x0
transportf
  (mor_disp ((ff ;; (hh ;; ii)) x0 xx)
     ((gg ;; hh ;; ii) x0 xx))
  (nat_trans_eq_pointwise (! rwhisker_rwhisker h i η)
     x0)
  (((ηη ▹▹ hh ;; ii) •• disp_lassociator gg hh ii) x0
     xx) =

  xx

! id_left (id₁ (i (h (g (f x0))))) @
nat_trans_eq_pointwise
  (! lassociator_lassociator f g h i) x0 =
! functor_id i (h (g (f x0))) @
! id_left ((# (pr1 i))%cat (id₁ (h (g (f x0))))) @
! id_left
    (id₁ (i (h (g (f x0))))
     · (# (pr1 i))%cat (id₁ (h (g (f x0))))) @
assoc (id₁ (i (h (g (pr1 f x0)))))
  (id₁ (i (h (g (f x0)))))
  ((# (pr1 i))%cat (id₁ (h (g (f x0)))))
 apply homset_property.

Definition disp_prebicat_of_univ_disp_cats
  : disp_prebicat bicat_of_univ_cats
  := _ ,, disp_prebicat_of_univ_disp_cats_laws.


disp_bicat bicat_of_univ_cats


disp_bicat bicat_of_univ_cats

  
disp_prebicat bicat_of_univ_cats
(λ D : disp_prebicat bicat_of_univ_cats,
 has_disp_cellset D) ?pr1

  
disp_prebicat bicat_of_univ_cats
 exact disp_prebicat_of_univ_disp_cats.
  
(λ D : disp_prebicat bicat_of_univ_cats,
 has_disp_cellset D) disp_prebicat_of_univ_disp_cats
 abstract
      (intros C₁ C₂ F₁ F₂ n D₁ D₂ FF₁ FF₂ ;
       simpl in * ;
       cbn ;
       exact (@isaset_disp_nat_trans C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F₁ F₂ n FF₁ FF₂)).
Defined.

(**
 2. Invertible 2-cells in the displayed bicategory of displayed categories
 *)

C, C': bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C, C' ⟧
D: disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C
D': disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C'
FF, GG: D -->[ F] D'
αα: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hαα: is_disp_nat_z_iso (nat_z_iso_id F) αα
is_disp_invertible_2cell (id2_invertible_2cell F) αα

αα: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hαα: is_disp_nat_z_iso (nat_z_iso_id F) αα
is_disp_invertible_2cell (id2_invertible_2cell F) αα

  
C, C': bicat_of_univ_cats

D: disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C
D': disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C'
FF, GG: D -->[ F] D'
αα: FF ==>[ id₂ F] GG
Hαα: is_disp_nat_z_iso (nat_z_iso_id F) αα
GG ==>[ (id2_invertible_2cell F) ^-1] FF

fiberwise_local_univalent disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats

  (disp_idtoiso_2_1 disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats
     (idpath F) FF GG)

transportf
  (λ z : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧, D₁ -->[ z] D₂)
  (idpath F) FF = GG
≃ disp_invertible_2cell (idtoiso_2_1 F F (idpath F))
    FF GG

FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
transportf
  (λ z : bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧, D₁ -->[ z] D₂)
  (idpath F) FF = GG
≃ disp_invertible_2cell (idtoiso_2_1 F F (idpath F))
    FF GG
 exact (disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats_inv2cell_weq FF GG
           ∘ disp_functor_eq_weq FF GG (pr2 D₂))%weq.

D₂: disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C₂
FF, GG: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
(disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats_inv2cell_weq FF GG
 ∘ disp_functor_eq_weq FF GG (pr2 D₂))%weq ~
disp_idtoiso_2_1 disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats
  (idpath F) FF GG
 abstract
      (intro p ;
       cbn in p ;
       induction p ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isaprop_is_disp_invertible_2cell | ] ;
       use disp_nat_trans_eq ;
       intros x xx ;
       cbn ;
       apply idpath).

      (cbn ;

                _ _

    apply isaprop_is_univalent_disp.
  
C: bicat_of_univ_cats
D₁, D₂: disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats C
(disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats_adjequiv_weq D₁ D₂
 ∘ univ_disp_cat_eq (pr1 D₁) (pr1 D₂) (pr2 D₁)
     (pr2 D₂)
 ∘ path_sigma_hprop is_univalent_disp D₁ D₂
     (isaprop_is_univalent_disp (pr1 D₂)))%weq ~
disp_idtoiso_2_0 disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cats
  (idpath C) D₁ D₂
 abstract
      (intro p ;
       cbn in p ;
       induction p ;
       use subtypePath ;
       [ intro ;
         use (isaprop_disp_left_adjoint_equivalence
                _ _
                univalent_cat_is_univalent_2_1
                disp_univalent_2_1_disp_bicat_of_univ_disp_cat)
       | ] ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

C, C': bicat_of_univ_cats

  (pr2
     (make_z_iso' (pr1 α x)
        (is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso α Hα x)))
  (id_disp (pr1 GG x xx))
 abstract
        (unfold transportb ;
         etrans ; [ apply (maponpaths (λ z, pr11 z x xx) (pr22 Hαα)) |] ;
         unfold transportb ;
         etrans ;
         [ refine (maponpaths (λ z, pr1 z x xx) _) ;
           exact (pr1_transportf
                    (!(vcomp_linv Hα))
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 GG),, tt))
         | ];
         etrans ;
         [ exact (@disp_nat_trans_transportf
                    _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _
                    (!(vcomp_linv Hα))
                    _ _
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 GG))
                    x xx)
         | ] ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         apply homset_property).

     (make_z_iso' (pr1 α x)

  (id_disp (pr1 GG x xx))

C, C': bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C, C' ⟧
α: F ==> G
Hα: is_invertible_2cell α
D: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C
D': disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C'
FF: D -->[ F] D'
GG: D -->[ G] D'
αα: FF ==>[ α] GG
Hαα: is_disp_invertible_2cell Hα αα
x: C : univalent_category
xx: (pr1 D : disp_univalent_category C) x
(pr111 Hαα) x xx ;; (pr11 αα) x xx =
transportb (mor_disp (pr1 GG x xx) (pr1 GG x xx))
  (pr2
     (make_z_iso' (pr1 α x)
        (is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso α Hα x)))
  (id_disp (pr1 GG x xx))
 abstract
        (unfold transportb ;
         etrans ; [ apply (maponpaths (λ z, pr11 z x xx) (pr22 Hαα)) |] ;
         unfold transportb ;
         etrans ;
         [ refine (maponpaths (λ z, pr1 z x xx) _) ;
           exact (pr1_transportf
                    (!(vcomp_linv Hα))
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 GG),, tt))
         | ];
         etrans ;
         [ exact (@disp_nat_trans_transportf
                    _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _
                    (!(vcomp_linv Hα))
                    _ _
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 GG))
                    x xx)
         | ] ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         apply homset_property).
    
C, C': bicat_of_univ_cats
F, G: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C, C' ⟧
α: F ==> G
Hα: is_invertible_2cell α
D: disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C
D': disp_bicat_of_opcleaving C'
FF: D -->[ F] D'
GG: D -->[ G] D'
αα: FF ==>[ α] GG
Hαα: is_disp_invertible_2cell Hα αα
x: C : univalent_category
xx: (pr1 D : disp_univalent_category C) x
(pr11 αα) x xx ;; (pr111 Hαα) x xx =
transportb (mor_disp (pr1 FF x xx) (pr1 FF x xx))
  (pr1
     (make_z_iso' (pr1 α x)
        (is_invertible_2cell_to_is_nat_z_iso α Hα x)))
  (id_disp (pr1 FF x xx))
 abstract
        (unfold transportb ;
         etrans ; [ apply (maponpaths (λ z, pr11 z x xx) (pr12 Hαα)) |] ;
         unfold transportb ;
         etrans ;
         [ refine (maponpaths (λ z, pr1 z x xx) _) ;
           exact (pr1_transportf
                    (!(vcomp_rinv Hα))
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 FF),, tt))
         | ] ;
         etrans ;
         [ exact (@disp_nat_trans_transportf
                    _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _
                    (!(vcomp_rinv Hα))
                    _ _
                    (disp_nat_trans_id (pr11 FF))
                    x xx)
         | ] ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         apply homset_property).
Defined.
